Those with the power of Illumination believe that light is the natural state of all things, and are devoted to focusing light on the world and ending the Midnight Age. An Illuminations adept works hard to attain a communion with the pure essence of light inherent in himself and the world around him. Once gained, the adept can draw on that attunement to affect the world around him, to banish the darkness from the world and bring forth a new Aetolian dawn. To aid in this attunement, the guild maintains a spectral flame in the guildhall, imbued with the concentrated power of light. Torchbearers for the light, the bringers of Illumination are the first heralds of the end of the Midnight Age.
